---

## Description
Wire types 是 Protobuf wire format 中的核心标识机制，每个字段在序列化时都会携带一个 wire type 标记，用于指示其后的数据采用何种编码方式。不同的 wire type 对应不同的编码格式：例如 wire type 2 表示 length-prefixed（定长前缀）编码，是 message 类型字段默认的编码方式；wire type 3/4 则用于 delimited（定界）编码，历史上对应 group 语法。在 editions 中，group 语法被正式废弃，但其编码行为通过 `features.message_encoding = DELIMITED` 得以保留，使得 message 类型字段能够以 group 编码（wire type 3/4）而非默认的 length-prefixed 编码（wire type 2）进行序列化。这一设计反映了"groups are funny message fields"这一现有 API 的实际情况，并简化了解析器的实现逻辑。Wire type 仅占 3 个比特，因此 field number 被限制在 29 位以内（而非完整的 32 位）。理解 wire type 对于理解 Protobuf 的二进制编码、packed encoding、group 编码以及 wire-format 与 API 兼容性之间的关系至关重要。

## Mentions in Source
> **Source: [[sources/editions|editions]]**
> - "The protobuf wire format is lean and doesn't provide a way to detect fields encoded using one definition and decoded using another."
> - "Reusing a field number makes decoding wire-format messages ambiguous."
> - "The field number is limited to 29 bits rather than 32 bits because three bits are used to specify the field's wire format."
> - "Singular fields can appear more than once in wire-format bytes."
> - "The parser will accept the input, but only the last instance of that field will be accessible through the generated bindings."
> - "See Last One Wins for more on this topic."

> **Source: [[sources/editions|editions]]**
> - No directly relevant information found in this source regarding Last One Wins.

> **Source: [[sources/editions-group-migration-issues|editions-group-migration-issues]]**
> - "The migration story for users is unclear. Overriding the value of this feature is both a "wire"-breaking and API-breaking change they may not be able to do easily."
> - "By updating the parsers to accept both, we have a migration path to change the "wire"-format"
> - No directly relevant information found in this source.

> **Source: [[sources/editions-edition-zero-features|editions-edition-zero-features]]**
> - "message-typed fields that have features.message_encoding = DELIMITED set will be encoded as groups (wire type 3/4) rather than byte blobs (wire type 2)"
> - "This reflects the existing API (groups are funny message fields) and simplifies the parser."
